This unique shape of the teardrop banners ensures that there is no additional fabric to flap in the wind which results in no fraying and significantly lengthens the life span of the product. It is a highly visible and eye catching product and can be displayed in any weather condition. Teardrop banners are lightweight, portable, and extremely easy to assemble. The trinodal pole can be adjusted like a fishing rod to ensure the perfect banner height. 
 An additional feature with the teardrop banners is that they can be printed on both sides. When you choose this option the two printed faces are bonded onto a light blocking layer which is highly beneficial as it eliminates any mirror images of your logo. If desired, you can also have different images printed on either side of the banner. Our teardrop banners come in three popular sizes to match your specific needs.

 Teardrop banners (also known as teardrop flags) are a distinctive and innovative flag banner product with the defining feature of the teardrop shape. This unique shape of the teardrop banners ensures that there is no additional fabric to flap in the wind which results in no fraying and significantly lengthens the life span of the product. It is a highly visible and eye catching product and can be displayed in any weather condition. Teardrop banners are lightweight, portable, and extremely easy to assemble. The trinodal pole can be adjusted like a fishing rod to ensure the perfect banner height. 
 An additional feature with the teardrop banners is that they can be printed on both sides. When you choose this option the two printed faces are bonded onto a light blocking layer which is highly beneficial as it eliminates any mirror images of your logo. If desired, you can also have different images printed on either side of the banner. Our teardrop banners come in three popular sizes to match your specific needs.

               <a href="http://www.youprint.ie/445-teardrop-banner-flags" title="Email us for a quote on cs@youprint.ie or call us on 022-32123   
 Teardrop banners (also known as teardrop flags) are a distinctive and innovative flag banner product with the defining feature of the teardrop shape. This unique shape of the teardrop banners ensures that there is no additional fabric to flap in the wind which results in no fraying and significantly lengthens the life span of the product. It is a highly visible and eye catching product and can be displayed in any weather condition. Teardrop banners are lightweight, portable, and extremely easy to assemble. The trinodal pole can be adjusted like a fishing rod to ensure the perfect banner height. 
 An additional feature with the teardrop banners is that they can be printed on both sides. When you choose this option the two printed faces are bonded onto a light blocking layer which is highly beneficial as it eliminates any mirror images of your logo. If desired, you can also have different images printed on either side of the banner. Our teardrop banners come in three popular sizes to match your specific needs.
